<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предание.html>преда́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предание.html>преда́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предание.html>преда́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предание.html>преда́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>handing over, committing</li>
<li>legend; tradition</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>to give oneself up <i>(to)</i>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:порок.html>поро́кам</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predátʹsja</b> porókam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to indulge in vices</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:предаться.html>преда́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>predátʹsja</b> mečtám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall into a reverie; lapse into daydreams</span></div></dd></dl></li>

***предварить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a> (30733)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пред-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pred-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:варить.html>вари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">varítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварять.html>предваря́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forestall, to anticipate</li>
<li>to premise <i>(with)</i>, to begin <i>(by)</i></li>
<li>to tell beforehand <i>(about)</i>, (fore)to warn <i>(of)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварительный.html>предвари́тельный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predvarítelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварительный.html>предвари́тельно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predvarítelʹno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">предвари́тельность</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">predvarítelʹnostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предварять.html>предваря́ть</a> (29736)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">predvarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварять.html>предваря́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predvarjátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предварить.html>предвари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forestall, to anticipate</li>
<li>to premise <i>(with)</i>, to begin <i>(by)</i></li>
<li>to tell beforehand <i>(about)</i>, (fore)to warn <i>(of)</i></li></ol>

***предел.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́л</a> (1428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́л</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">predél</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́ла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́лы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предел.html>преде́лов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>limit, boundary, margin</li>
<li>border</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the plural</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> precincts</li>
